     <p> A cave squats near the bank of a putrid lagoon, its entrance almost obscured by the cloud of flies filling the air. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('1wqOmGYr');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> <strong> 3 Giant Crocodiles</strong> are foraging on a dry patch of land. </p> <p> Theres a <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d6' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d6');"><strong>2-in-6</strong></a> chance of encountering at least some of them outside (the rest will be in their lair inside a well-hidden cave). </p> <p> <strong>Giant Crocodile</strong>   <hr/> <div id="block-1wqOmGYr" class="monster-block"> <div class="statblock"> <div class="statblock-top-row"> <div><span class="section-label">CR:</span> 5 (1800 XP)</div> <div><span class="section-label">AC:</span> 14 (natural armor)</div> <div><span class="section-label">HP:</span>  (9d12 + 27)</div> <div><span class="section-label">Speed:</span> Walk 30 ft. Swim 50 ft.</div> </div> <table class="statblock-table"> <tr><th>STR</th><th>DEX</th><th>CON</th><th>INT</th><th>WIS</th><th>CHA</th></tr> <tr> <td>21 <small> +6 </small> </td> <td>9 <small> -1 </small> </td> <td>17 <small> +4 </small> </td> <td>2 <small> -4 </small> </td> <td>10 <small>  </small> </td> <td>7 <small> -2 </small> </td> </tr> </table> <div> <input class="monster-block-toggle" name="toggle-1wqOmGYr" id="toggle-1wqOmGYr" type="checkbox" onclick="javascript:document.getElementById('block-1wqOmGYr').scrollIntoView();"/> <div id="block-toggle-1wqOmGYr" class="statblock-container"> <ul>      </ul>  <hr/> <div><ul> <li><strong>Hold Breath:</strong> The crocodile can hold its breath for 30 minutes.</li> </ul></div>   <hr/> <h6>Actions</h6> <div><ul> <li><strong>Multiattack:</strong> The crocodile makes two attacks: one with its bite and one with its tail.</li><li><strong>Bite:</strong> <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d20+8' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d20+8');"><strong><strong>+8</strong></strong></a> to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. Inflicts 21 (<a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='3d10 + 5' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('3d10 + 5');"><strong>3d10 + 5</strong></a>) piercing damage, and the target is <strong>grappled</strong> (escape <strong>DC16</strong>).
